The Real Charles Dawes

While I initially felt like I should put some humorous ending in for those of you who have “bigshotted” your way into finding this, I decided instead to encourage those of you interested in Charles Dawes to learn more. In our universe, Charles Dawes served with distinction in that great and terrible war of 1914–1918 and would go on to win the Nobel Peace Prize and serve as Vice President before returning to his bank in Illinois, where he kept it solvent through the Great Depression. He also composed a hit song.

While I personally disagree with a number of Dawes’ personal views, I believe he was a truly extraordinary man, whose talent as a diplomat, soldier, banker, politician, and musician dwarfed most others. Honestly, I’m not entirely sure I fully did him justice. If you want to learn more about him, I’d recommend reading “Portrait of an American: Charles Dawes,” which, while out of print, is easily accessible online.
